   171 function MessageBubble({ message, onAnswerPermission, onAnswerUser, onEditUserMessage }: {
   172   message: Message;
   173   onAnswerPermission?: (stepIndex: number, answer: 'once' | 'session' | 'deny') => void;
   174   onAnswerUser?: (stepIndex: number, answers: Record<string, string>) => void;
   175   onEditUserMessage?: (content: string) => void;
   176 }) {
   177   const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);
   178   const isUser = message.role === 'user';
   179   const isComplete = message.is_complete ?? true;
   180 
   181   const handleCopy = () => {
   182     navigator.clipboard.writeText(message.content);
   183     setCopied(true);
   184     setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 2000);
   185   };
   186 
   187   const renderContent = (content: string) => {
   188     const parts = content.split(/(```[\s\S]*?```)/g);
   189     return parts.map((part, i) => {
   190       if (part.startsWith('```') && part.endsWith('```')) {
   191         const lines = part.slice(3, -3).split('\n');
   192         const lang = lines[0]?.trim() || '';
   193         const code = lines.slice(lang ? 1 : 0).join('\n');
   194         return (
   195           <div key={i} className="my-2 rounded overflow-hidden border border-border">
   196             <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-1.5 bg-secondary/50 border-b border-border">
   197               <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground font-mono">{lang}</span>
   198               <button type="button" onClick={handleCopy} className="text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors">{copied ? <Check className="w-3 h-3" /> : <Copy className="w-3 h-3" />}</button>
   199             </div>
   200             <pre className="p-3 text-xs font-mono leading-relaxed overflow-x-auto bg-background/50"><code>{code}</code></pre>
   201           </div>
   202         );
   203       }
   204       return part.split('\n').map((line, j) => (
   205         <span key={`${i}-${j}`}>{line}{j < part.split('\n').length - 1 && <br />}</span>
   206       ));
   207     });
   208   };
   209 
   210   if (isUser) {
   211     return (
   212       <div className="flex gap-3 px-4 py-3 justify-end group">
   213         <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 max-w-[85%]">
   214           <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-2 mb-1">
   215             <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">你</span>
   216           </div>
   217           <div className="bg-primary/15 rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5 text-sm text-foreground leading-relaxed">{renderContent(message.content)}</div>
   218           {/* 用户消息底部操作按钮 */}
   219           <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1.5 mt-1.5 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity">
   220             <button
   221               type="button"
   222               onClick={handleCopy}
   223               className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded hover:bg-secondary/50"
   224             >
   225               {copied ? <Check className="w-3 h-3" /> : <Copy className="w-3 h-3" />}
   226               复制
   227             </button>
   228             <button
   229               type="button"
   230               onClick={() => onEditUserMessage?.(message.content)}
   231               className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded hover:bg-secondary/50"
   232             >
   233               <Pencil className="w-3 h-3" />
   234               编辑
   235             </button>
   236           </div>
   237         </div>
   238         <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded shrink-0 flex items-center justify-center bg-primary/20"><User className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-primary" /></div>
   239       </div>
   240     );
   241   }
   242 
   243   // AI消息
   244   return (
   245     <div className="flex gap-3 px-4 py-3">
   246       <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded shrink-0 flex items-center justify-center bg-accent relative">
   247         <Bot className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-primary" />
   248         {!isComplete && (
   249           <div className="absolute -bottom-0.5 -right-0.5 w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full bg-primary border-2 border-background animate-pulse" />
   250         )}

    85 // 根据扩展名返回图标
    86 function getFileIcon(path: string) {
    87   if (path.endsWith('.tsx') || path.endsWith('.ts') || path.endsWith('.jsx') || path.endsWith('.js')) return Braces;
    88   if (path.endsWith('.css') || path.endsWith('.scss') || path.endsWith('.less')) return Hash;
    89   if (path.endsWith('.json')) return FileJson;
    90   if (path.endsWith('.html') || path.endsWith('.htm')) return Globe;
    91   if (path.endsWith('.md')) return FileText;
    92   if (path.endsWith('.png') || path.endsWith('.jpg') || path.endsWith('.svg') || path.endsWith('.jpeg')) return FileImage;
    93   if (path.endsWith('.java')) return Coffee;
    94   if (path.endsWith('.config.ts') || path.endsWith('.config.js')) return Settings;
    95   return FileCode2;
    96 }
    97

```
  // 拖拽拉伸
  const handleResizeStart = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    setIsResizing(true);
    resizeStartX.current = e.clientX;
    resizeStartWidth.current = panelWidth;
  }, [panelWidth]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isResizing) return;
      const delta = e.clientX - resizeStartX.current;
      const newWidth = Math.max(180, Math.min(400, resizeStartWidth.current + delta));
      setPanelWidth(newWidth);
    };
    const handleMouseUp = () => setIsResizing(false);
    if (isResizing) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
      document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
    }
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      document.body.style.cursor = '';
      document.body.style.userSelect = '';
    };
  }, [isResizing]);
```

```
  // 编辑用户消息（将内容填入输入区域）
  const handleEditUserMessage = (content: string) => {
    setEditContent(content);
    toast.info('已加载到输入框，你可以修改后重新发送');
  };

  // 重试失败的步骤
  const handleRetryStep = (messageId: string, stepIndex: number) => {
    toast.success('正在重试...');
    setMessages((prev) =>
      prev.map((msg) => {
        if (msg.id !== messageId || !msg.steps) return msg;
        const newSteps = [...msg.steps];
        if (newSteps[stepIndex]) {
          newSteps[stepIndex] = { ...newSteps[stepIndex], failed: false, type: 'tool_use' };
        }
        return { ...msg, steps: newSteps };
      })
    );
  };

  // 退出登录
```

```
        type: 'tool_use',
        content: `尝试写入文件...`,
        toolName: 'apply_diff',
        summary: { file: 'src/components/App.tsx', lines: 8, durationMs: 560 },
        failed: true,
      } : {
        type: 'tool_use',
        content: `正在生成代码补丁...`,
        toolName: 'apply_diff',
        summary: { file: 'src/components/App.tsx', lines: 8, durationMs: 560 },
      },
      shouldFail ? {
        type: 'tool_result',
        content: `写入失败：权限不足，无法修改 src/components/App.tsx`,
        toolName: 'apply_diff',
        failed: true,
      } : {
        type: 'tool_result',
        content: `文件写入成功。`,
        toolName: 'apply_diff',
        summary: { file: 'src/components/App.tsx', lines: 8, durationMs: 560 },
        diff: `diff --git a/src/components/App.tsx b/src/components/App.tsx\n--- a/src/components/App.tsx\n+++ b/src/components/App.tsx\n@@ -1,5 +1,8 @@\n import React from "react";\n+import { useState } from "react";\n \n-export default function App() {\n+export default function App(): JSX.Element {\n+  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);\n   return <div>Hello World</div>;\n }`,
      },
      {
        type: 'ask_user',
        content: '为了更好地实现功能，请回答以下问题：',
        questions: [
          { id: 'q1', label: '你希望使用哪种状态管理方案？', type: 'choice', options: ['React Context', 'Zustand', 'Redux Toolkit', 'Jotai'] },
          { id: 'q2', label: '样式方案偏好', type: 'choice', options: ['Tailwind CSS', 'CSS Modules', 'Styled Components', 'SCSS'] },
        ],
      },
    ];

    if (shouldCompress) {
      steps.push({
        type: 'compress',
        content: '正在压缩生成的资源文件...',
        compressInfo: { originalSize: 12480, compressedSize: 4320, ratio: 0.346, status: 'compressing' },
      });
      steps.push({
        type: 'compress',
        content: '资源压缩完成',
        compressInfo: { originalSize: 12480, compressedSize: 4320, ratio: 0.346, status: 'done' },
      });
    }

    steps.push({
      type: 'final',
      content: `已完成你的需求！我分析了项目结构并生成了相应的代码。\n\n主要改动：\n1. 创建了新组件\n2. 更新了相关页面\n3. 添加了必要的样式\n\n\`\`\`typescript\n// 示例代码\nfunction implementFeature() {\n  console.log("功能已实现");\n  return true;\n}\n\`\`\`\n\n你可以在右侧「变更」面板查看修改的文件列表，在「任务」面板跟踪进度。`,
    });

    const finalContent = steps[steps.length - 1].content;
    const token_in = Math.floor(userMsg.length * 0.8) + Math.floor(Math.random() * 200);
    const token_out = Math.floor(finalContent.length * 0.9) + Math.floor(Math.random() * 300);
    return { steps, finalContent, token_in, token_out };
  };
```

```
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
                    输入 <span className="text-foreground font-medium">{totalIn.toLocaleString()}</span> tokens
                  </span>
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
                    输出 <span className="text-foreground font-medium">{totalOut.toLocaleString()}</span> tokens
                  </span>
                </>
              );
            })()}
          </div>
        </div>
```

    45 
    46 function generateName(existing: string[]): string {
    47   const available = defaultNames.filter((n) => !existing.includes(n));
    48   if (available.length > 0) {
    49     return available[Math.floor(Math.random() * available.length)];
    50   }
    51   // 随机生成3字以内的名字
    52   const chars = '小阿明红宇强琳凯慧杰燕峰龙雪伟芳文武涛静超磊洋敏';
    53   const len = 2 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 2); // 2或3字
    54   let name = '';
    55   for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) {
    56     name += chars[Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length)];
    57   }
    58   return name;
    59 }

```
export default function AddAgentDialog({ open, onOpenChange, onAddAgent, existingNames }: AddAgentDialogProps) {
  const [selectedAgent, setSelectedAgent] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [displayName, setDisplayName] = useState('');
  const [workspace, setWorkspace] = useState('.');

  // 每次打开时重置
  useEffect(() => {
    if (open) {
      setSelectedAgent(null);
      setDisplayName(generateName(existingNames));
      setWorkspace('.');
    }
  }, [open, existingNames]);

  const handleConfirm = () => {
    if (!selectedAgent) return;
    const trimmed = displayName.trim().slice(0, 3);
    const ws = workspace.trim() || '.';
    onAddAgent(selectedAgent, trimmed || generateName(existingNames), ws);
    onOpenChange(false);
  };
```

```
                    <span className={`w-5 h-5 rounded text-[10px] font-bold flex items-center justify-center ${config.bg} ${config.color}`}>
                      {config.letter}
                    </span>
                    <span className="flex-1 text-left truncate">{instance.displayName}</span>
                    {isActive && <span className="text-[10px] text-primary">当前</span>}
                  </button>
                );
              })}
            </PopoverContent>
          </Popover>
          <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate max-w-[200px]" title={activeAgent.workspace}>
            {activeAgent.workspace}
          </span>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
          <span>AI Coding v1.0</span>
        </div>
      </div>
```

    35 const defaultNames = ['小智', '阿明', '小红', '小宇', '阿强', '小琳', '小凯', '小慧', '阿杰', '小燕', '小峰', '阿丽', '小龙', '小雪', '阿伟', '小芳'];
    36 const nameChars = '小阿明红宇强琳凯慧杰燕峰龙雪伟芳文武涛静超磊洋敏';
    37 
    38 function generateName(existing: string[] = []): string {
    39   const available = defaultNames.filter((n) => !existing.includes(n));
    40   if (available.length > 0) {
    41     return available[Math.floor(Math.random() * available.length)];
    42   }
    43   const len = 2 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 2);
    44   let name = '';
    45   for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) {
    46     name += nameChars[Math.floor(Math.random() * nameChars.length)];
    47   }
    48   return name;
    49 }

   173 export default function SettingsDialog({ open, onOpenChange }: SettingsDialogProps) {
   174   const [agent, setAgent] = useState(localStorage.getItem('selected_agent') || 'opencode');

   180   const [activeTag, setActiveTag] = useState('全部');
   181 
   182   const handleSave = () => {
   183     localStorage.setItem('selected_agent', agent);
   184     toast.success('设置已保存');
   185     onOpenChange(false);
   186   };
   187 
   188   const filteredPrompts = promptCards.filter((card) => {
   189     const matchSearch = !promptSearch || card.title.includes(promptSearch) || card.content.includes(promptSearch);
   190     const matchTag = activeTag === '全部' || card.tags.includes(activeTag);
   191     return matchSearch && matchTag;
   192   });
   193 
   194   const [copiedId, setCopiedId] = useState<string | null>(null);
   195   const handleCopyPrompt = (card: { id: string; title: string; content: string }) => {
   196     navigator.clipboard.writeText(`${card.title}\n${card.content}`);
   197     setCopiedId(card.id);
   198     toast.success('提示词已复制');
   199     setTimeout(() => setCopiedId(null), 2000);
   200   };

   396                         <SelectItem value="cloud">云服务部署</SelectItem>
   397                         <SelectItem value="static">静态站点</SelectItem>
   398                       </SelectContent>
   399                     </Select>
   400                   </div>
   401                 </div>
   402               </div>
   403             )}
   404 
   405             {activeSetting === 'prompts' && (
   406               <div className="space-y-3">
   407                 <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
   408                   <FileText className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
   409                   <span className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">提示词库</span>
   410                 </div>
   411 
   412                 {/* 搜索 */}
   413                 <div className="relative">
   414                   <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
   415                   <Input
   416                     value={promptSearch}
   417                     onChange={(e) => setPromptSearch(e.target.value)}
   418                     placeholder="搜索提示词..."
   419                     className="pl-9 bg-secondary border-border text-sm h-8"
   420                   />
   421                   {promptSearch && (
   422                     <button
   423                       type="button"
   424                       onClick={() => setPromptSearch('')}
   425                       className="absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2"
   426                     >
   427                       <X className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground" />
   428                     </button>
   429                   )}
   430                 </div>
   431 
   432                 {/* 标签筛选 */}
   433                 <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
   434                   {allTags.map((tag) => (
   435                     <button
   436                       key={tag}
   437                       type="button"
   438                       onClick={() => setActiveTag(tag)}
   439                       className={`px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] rounded-full transition-colors ${
   440                         activeTag === tag
   441                           ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
   442                           : 'bg-secondary text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'
   443                       }`}
   444                     >
   445                       {tag}
   446                     </button>
   447                   ))}
   448                 </div>
   449 
   450                 {/* 提示词卡片 */}
   451                 <div className="space-y-2 max-h-[300px] overflow-y-auto">
   452                   {filteredPrompts.length === 0 ? (
   453                     <div className="text-center py-6 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   454                       未找到相关提示词
   455                     </div>
   456                   ) : (
   457                     filteredPrompts.map((card) => (
   458                       <div
   459                         key={card.id}
   460                         className="p-3 rounded border border-border bg-secondary/30 hover:bg-secondary/50 transition-colors"
   461                       >
   462                         <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
   463                           <h4 className="text-xs font-medium text-foreground">{card.title}</h4>
   464                           <div className="flex gap-1 shrink-0 items-center">
   465                             {card.tags.map((tag) => (
   466                               <Badge key={tag} variant="secondary" className="text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0 h-4">
   467                                 {tag}
   468                               </Badge>
   469                             ))}
   470                             <button
   471                               type="button"
   472                               onClick={() => handleCopyPrompt(card)}
   473                               className="ml-1 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors"
   474                             >
   475                               {copiedId === card.id ? (
   476                                 <Check className="w-3 h-3 text-green-400" />
   477                               ) : (
   478                                 <Copy className="w-3 h-3" />
   479                               )}
   480                             </button>
   481                           </div>
   482                         </div>
   483                         <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground mt-1.5 line-clamp-2">{card.content}</p>
   484                       </div>
   485                     ))
   486                   )}
   487                 </div>
   488               </div>
   489             )}
   490 
   491             {activeSetting === 'specs' && (
   492               <SpecsPanel />
   493             )}
   494 
   495             {activeSetting === 'mcp' && (
   496               <div className="space-y-4">
   497                 <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
   498                   <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   499                     <Plug className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
   500                     <span className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">MCP 服务器配置</span>
   501                   </div>
   502                   <button
   503                     type="button"
   504                     onClick={handleAddMcpServer}
   505                     className="flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 text-[11px] rounded bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90 transition-colors"
   506                   >
   507                     <Plus className="w-3 h-3" />
   508                     添加
   509                   </button>
   510                 </div>
   511                 <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">
   512                   Model Context Protocol (MCP) 允许智能体通过标准化接口与外部工具和数据源交互。
   513                 </p>
   514                 <div className="space-y-3 max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto">
   515                   {mcpServers.map((server) => (
   516                     <div key={server.id} className="rounded border border-border bg-secondary/30 p-3 space-y-2">
   517                       <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
   518                         <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   519                           <input
   520                             type="checkbox"
   521                             checked={server.enabled}
   522                             onChange={(e) => handleUpdateMcpServer(server.id, 'enabled', e.target.checked)}
   523                             className="w-3.5 h-3.5 rounded border-border accent-primary"
   524                           />
   525                           <span className="text-xs font-medium text-foreground">{server.name || '未命名'}</span>
   526                         </div>
   527                         <button
   528                           type="button"
   529                           onClick={() => handleRemoveMcpServer(server.id)}
   530                           className="text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive transition-colors"
   531                         >
   532                           <Trash2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
   533                         </button>
   534                       </div>
   535                       <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
   536                         <div className="space-y-1">
   537                           <Label className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">名称</Label>
   538                           <Input
   539                             value={server.name}
   540                             onChange={(e) => handleUpdateMcpServer(server.id, 'name', e.target.value)}
   541                             placeholder="server-name"
   542                             className="bg-secondary border-border text-xs h-7"
   543                           />
   544                         </div>
   545                         <div className="space-y-1">
   546                           <Label className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">命令</Label>
   547                           <Input
   548                             value={server.command}
   549                             onChange={(e) => handleUpdateMcpServer(server.id, 'command', e.target.value)}
   550                             placeholder="npx, uvx, python..."
   551                             className="bg-secondary border-border text-xs h-7"
   552                           />
   553                         </div>
   554                       </div>
   555                       <div className="space-y-1">
   556                         <Label className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">参数</Label>
   557                         <Input
   558                           value={server.args}
   559                           onChange={(e) => handleUpdateMcpServer(server.id, 'args', e.target.value)}
   560                           placeholder="-y @modelcontextprotocol/server-filesystem"
   561                           className="bg-secondary border-border text-xs h-7"
   562                         />
   563                       </div>
   564                       <div className="space-y-1">
   565                         <Label className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">环境变量</Label>
   566                         <Input
   567                           value={server.env}
   568                           onChange={(e) => handleUpdateMcpServer(server.id, 'env', e.target.value)}
   569                           placeholder="KEY=VALUE;KEY2=VALUE2"
   570                           className="bg-secondary border-border text-xs h-7"
   571                         />
   572                       </div>
   573                     </div>
   574                   ))}
   575                   {mcpServers.length === 0 && (
   576                     <div className="text-center py-8 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   577                       暂无MCP服务器，点击上方「添加」按钮创建
   578                     </div>
   579                   )}
   580                 </div>
   581               </div>
   582             )}
   583           </div>
   584         </div>
   585       </SheetContent>
   586     </Sheet>
   587   );
   588 }

Thought: 
Command: create
Created File with Text:
```
import { useRef } from 'react';
import { FolderOpen } from 'lucide-react';

interface DirectoryPickerButtonProps {
  onSelect: (path: string) => void;
}

export default function DirectoryPickerButton({ onSelect }: DirectoryPickerButtonProps) {
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  const handleClick = () => {
    inputRef.current?.click();
  };

  const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const files = e.target.files;
    if (files && files.length > 0) {
      // 取第一个文件的路径，提取目录部分
      const filePath = files[0].webkitRelativePath || files[0].name;
      const dirPath = filePath.includes('/') ? filePath.split('/')[0] : '.';
      onSelect(dirPath);
    }
    // 重置 input 以便可以重复选择同一目录
    if (inputRef.current) inputRef.current.value = '';
  };

  return (
    <>
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={handleClick}
        className="w-7 h-7 flex items-center justify-center rounded border border-border bg-secondary text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80 transition-colors shrink-0"
        title="选择文件夹"
      >
        <FolderOpen className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
      </button>
      <input
        ref={inputRef}
        type="file"
        webkitdirectory="true"
        directory=""
        onChange={handleChange}
        className="hidden"
      />
    </>
  );
}

```

```
            />
            <button

            </button>
```

```
  { key: 'green', label: '翡翠绿', hsl: '142 71% 45%', dot: 'bg-green-400' },

function applyThemeColor(colorKey: string) {
  const option = themeColorOptions.find((o) => o.key === colorKey);
  if (!option) return;
  const root = document.documentElement;
  root.style.setProperty('--primary', option.hsl);
  root.style.setProperty('--ring', option.hsl);
  root.style.setProperty('--chart-1', option.hsl);
  root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-primary', option.hsl);
  root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-ring', option.hsl);
  root.style.setProperty('--info', option.hsl);
  localStorage.setItem('theme_color', colorKey);
}

export default function SettingsDialog({ open, onOpenChange, agents, onUpdateAgents }: SettingsDialogProps) {
  const [model, setModel] = useState('gpt-4');
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState('dark');
  const [themeColor, setThemeColor] = useState(localStorage.getItem('theme_color') || 'blue');
  const [language, setLanguage] = useState(localStorage.getItem('app_language') || 'zh');
  const [skillDesign, setSkillDesign] = useState('auto');
  const [skillCode, setSkillCode] = useState('auto');
  const [promptSearch, setPromptSearch] = useState('');
  const [activeTag, setActiveTag] = useState('全部');

  // 加载保存的主题色
  useEffect(() => {
    if (open) {
      const saved = localStorage.getItem('theme_color') || 'blue';
      setThemeColor(saved);
    }
  }, [open]);

  const handleSave = () => {
    localStorage.setItem('app_language', language);
    toast.success('设置已保存');
    onOpenChange(false);
  };

  const handleThemeColorChange = (colorKey: string) => {
    setThemeColor(colorKey);
    applyThemeColor(colorKey);
  };

  const handleLanguageChange = (lang: string) => {
    setLanguage(lang);
    localStorage.setItem('app_language', lang);
  };
```

New String: ```
// 智能体模型配置卡片
function AgentModelCard({
  agent,
  onUpdate,
  allAgents,
}: {
  agent: AgentInstance;
  onUpdate: (agents: AgentInstance[]) => void;
  allAgents: AgentInstance[];
}) {
  const [showKey, setShowKey] = useState(false);
  const config = agent.modelConfig || { type: 'builtin', modelId: 'gpt-4' };

  const updateConfig = (patch: Partial<typeof config>) => {
    const newConfig = { ...config, ...patch };
    onUpdate(
      allAgents.map((a) =>
        a.id === agent.id ? { ...a, modelConfig: newConfig } : a
      )
    );
  };

  return (
    <div className="rounded-lg border border-border bg-secondary/20 p-3 space-y-3">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        <span className="text-xs font-medium text-foreground">{agent.displayName}</span>
        <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-[9px] px-1.5 h-4">
          {agent.agentKey}
        </Badge>
      </div>

      {/* 模型来源 */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        {[
          { key: 'builtin', label: '内置模型' },
          { key: 'custom', label: '自定义' },
        ].map((opt) => (
          <button
            key={opt.key}
            type="button"
            onClick={() => updateConfig({ type: opt.key as 'builtin' | 'custom' })}
            className={`px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] rounded border transition-colors ${
              config.type === opt.key
                ? 'border-primary bg-primary/10 text-primary'
                : 'border-border bg-secondary text-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80'
            }`}
          >
            {opt.label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {config.type === 'builtin' ? (
        <div className="space-y-1">
          <Label className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">选择模型</Label>
          <Select
            value={config.modelId || 'gpt-4'}
            onValueChange={(v) => updateConfig({ modelId: v })}
          >
            <SelectTrigger className="bg-secondary border-border text-xs h-8">
              <SelectValue />
            </SelectTrigger>
            <SelectContent>
              {builtinModels.map((m) => (
                <SelectItem key={m.id} value={m.id} className="text-xs">
                  {m.name}
                </SelectItem>
              ))}
            </SelectContent>
          </Select>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="space-y-2">
          <div className="space-y-1">
            <Label className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">模型名称</Label>
            <Input
              value={config.name || ''}
              onChange={(e) => updateConfig({ name: e.target.value })}
              placeholder="例如：自定义 GPT"
              className="bg-secondary border-border text-xs h-8"
            />
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-1">
            <Label className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">API URL</Label>
            <Input
              value={config.url || ''}
              onChange={(e) => updateConfig({ url: e.target.value })}
              placeholder="https://api.example.com/v1/chat/completions"
              className="bg-secondary border-border text-xs h-8"
            />
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-1">
            <Label className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">API KEY</Label>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
              <Input
                type={showKey ? 'text' : 'password'}
                value={config.apiKey || ''}
                onChange={(e) => updateConfig({ apiKey: e.target.value })}
                placeholder="sk-..."
                className="bg-secondary border-border text-xs h-8"
              />
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => setShowKey(!showKey)}
                className="w-8 h-8 flex items-center justify-center rounded border border-border bg-secondary text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors shrink-0"
                title={showKey ? '隐藏' : '显示'}
              >
                {showKey ? <EyeOff className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> : <Eye className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import IntersectObserver from '@/components/common/IntersectObserver';
import { Toaster } from '@/components/ui/sonner';
import { AuthProvider } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';

import { routes } from './routes';

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <Router>
      <AuthProvider>
        <IntersectObserver />
        <Routes>
          {routes.map((route, index) => (
            <Route
              key={index}
              path={route.path}
              element={route.element}
            />
          ))}
          <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/login" replace />} />
        </Routes>
        <Toaster />
      </AuthProvider>
    </Router>
  );
};

export default App;

New String: ```
import React, { useEffect } from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import IntersectObserver from '@/components/common/IntersectObserver';
import { Toaster } from '@/components/ui/sonner';
import { AuthProvider } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';

import { routes } from './routes';

const themeColorMap: Record<string, string> = {
  blue: '213 94% 68%',
  green: '142 71% 45%',
  orange: '25 95% 53%',
  purple: '270 60% 55%',
  pink: '340 75% 55%',
};

const App: React.FC = () => {
  useEffect(() => {
    const savedColor = localStorage.getItem('theme_color') || 'blue';
    const hsl = themeColorMap[savedColor] || themeColorMap.blue;
    const root = document.documentElement;
    root.style.setProperty('--primary', hsl);
    root.style.setProperty('--ring', hsl);
    root.style.setProperty('--chart-1', hsl);
    root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-primary', hsl);
    root.style.setProperty('--sidebar-ring', hsl);
    root.style.setProperty('--info', hsl);
  }, []);

  return (
    <Router>
      <AuthProvider>
        <IntersectObserver />
        <Routes>
          {routes.map((route, index) => (
            <Route
              key={index}
              path={route.path}
              element={route.element}
            />
          ))}
          <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/login" replace />} />
        </Routes>
        <Toaster />
      </AuthProvider>
    </Router>
  );
};

export default App;
```

  interface MCPServer {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    command: string;
    args: string;
    env: string;
    enabled: boolean;
  }
  const [mcpServers, setMcpServers] = useState<MCPServer[]>([
    { id: '1', name: 'filesystem', command: 'npx', args: '-y @modelcontextprotocol/server-filesystem /path/to/project', env: '', enabled: true },
    { id: '2', name: 'github', command: 'npx', args: '-y @modelcontextprotocol/server-github', env: 'GITHUB_TOKEN=your_token', enabled: false },
  ]);
  const handleAddMcpServer = () => {
    const newServer: MCPServer = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      name: '',
      command: '',
      args: '',
      env: '',
      enabled: true,
    };
    setMcpServers((prev) => [...prev, newServer]);
  };
  const handleRemoveMcpServer = (id: string) => {
    setMcpServers((prev) => prev.filter((s) => s.id !== id));
  };
  const handleUpdateMcpServer = (id: string, field: keyof MCPServer, value: string | boolean) => {
    setMcpServers((prev) => prev.map((s) => (s.id === id ? { ...s, [field]: value } : s)));
  };

  return (
    <Sheet open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
      <SheetContent side="right" className="w-screen sm:w-screen p-0 bg-card border-l border-border overflow-hidden">

          <SheetTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-foreground">
            <Settings className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
            设置
          </SheetTitle>
        </SheetHeader>

          {/* 左侧菜单 */}
          <div className="w-40 shrink-0 border-r border-border bg-secondary/30">
